append(noop, change)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t// Handle other actions (Read, Forget, etc.)\n\t\t\tnoop = append(noop, change)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Sort each group for consistent output\n\tsortChanges(creates)\n\tsortChanges(updates)\n\tsortChanges(deletes)\n\tsortChanges(replaces)\n\n\t// Output changes grouped by action type\n\tif len(creates) > 0 {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Create\\n\")\n\t\tfor _, change := range creates {\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  [+] %s\\n\", change.Addr.String()))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif len(updates) > 0 {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Update\\n\")\n\t\tfor _, change := range updates {\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  [~] %s\\n\", change.Addr.String()))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif len(replaces) > 0 {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Delete\\n\")\n\t\tfor _, change := range deletes {\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  [-] %s\\n\", change.Addr.String()))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Summary count\n\ttotal := len(creates) + len(updates) + len(replaces) + len(deletes)\n\tif total > 0 {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"Plan: %d to add, %d to change, %d to destroy.\\n\",\n\t\t\tlen(creates), len(updates)+len(replaces), len(deletes)))\n\t}\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n\n// sortChanges sorts changes by their address for consistent output\nfunc sortChanges(changes plan as a compact summary of resource changes.\n// Changes are grouped by action type (Create, Update, Delete, Replace)\n// and a summary count is shown at the end.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\t// Group changes by action\n\tcreates := []*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc{}\n\tupdates := []*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc{}\n\tdeletes := []*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc{}\n\treplaces := []*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc{}\n\tnoop := []*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc{}\n\n\tfor _, change := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\t// Skip deposed objects (only format the current object)\n\t\tif change.DeposedKey != states.NotDeposed {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tswitch change.Action {\n\t\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\t\tcreates = append(creates, change)\n\t\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\t\tupdates = append(updates, change)\n\t\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\t\tdeletes = append(deletes, change)\n\t\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate, plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\t\treplaces = append(replaces, change)\n\t\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\t\tnoop = append(noop, change)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t// Handle other actions (Read, Forget, etc.)\n\t\t\tnoop = append(noop, change)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Sort each group for consistent output\n\tsortChanges(creates)\n\tsortChanges(updates)\n\tsortChanges(deletes)\n\tsortChanges(replaces)\n\n\t// Output changes grouped by action type\n\tif len(creates) > 0 {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Create\\n\")\n\t\tfor _, change := range creates {\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  [+] %s\\n\", change.Addr.String()))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif len(updates) > 0 {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Update\\n\")\n\t\tfor _, change := range updates {\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  [~] %s\\n\", change.Addr.String()))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif len(replaces) > 0 {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Replace\\n\")\n\t\tfor _, change := range replaces {\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  [-/+] %s\\n\", change.Addr.String()))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif len(deletes) > 0 {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Delete\\n\")\n\t\tfor _, change := range deletes {\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  [-] %s\\n\", change.Addr.String()))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Summary count\n\ttotal := len(creates) + len(updates) + len(replaces) + len(deletes)\n\tif total > 0 {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"Plan: %d to add, %d to change, %d to destroy.\\n\",\n\t\t\tlen(creates), len(updates)+len(replaces), len(deletes)))\n\t}\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n\n// sortChanges sorts changes by their address for consistent output\nfunc sortChanges(changes []*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc) {\n\tsort.Slice(changes, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\treturn changes[i].Addr.String() < changes[j].Addr.String()\n\t})\n}\n\n// FormatCompactDiff is a convenience function that creates a CompactDiffFormatter\n// and formats the given plan.\nfunc FormatCompactDiff(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tformatter := &CompactDiffFormatter{}\n\treturn formatter.Format(plan, schemas)\n}\n","numLines":120,"startLine":1,"totalLines":120}}}
